### ğŸ° **What Vegas Odds Actually Mean (Plain English Version):**

Vegas odds are how bookmakers **predict the likelihood** of something happeningâ€”and how much you'd win if you bet on it.

â¡ï¸ Translation: **Still possible, but not the favorite.**
